## SECTION 11: GTM & COMPLIANCE MODULE – STRATEGIC PARTNERS \+ BDCS

### 11.1 Overview: Two-Layer GTM Strategy

Cuboid's Go-to-Market strategy has two parallel layers that serve different constituencies while maintaining a unified platform. This section covers the **GTM & Compliance Module** – the set of features, partnerships, and processes that make Cuboid regulator-friendly while enabling strategic partnerships with BDCs, banks, and fintechs.

**The two layers summarized:**

| Layer | Primary Audience | Goal | Timeline |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Broker Layer** | Informal brokers (bank workers, agents) | Drive volume, demonstrate utility | Months 0–6 (stealth) |
| **Compliance & Partner Layer** | BDCs, regulators, banks, fintechs | Formalize volume, generate revenue, gain regulatory acceptance | Months 3–12 |

**The GTM & Compliance Module is the bridge between these layers.** It provides the tools that licensed BDCs need to participate (compliance, reporting, inter-trading) and the features that make Cuboid attractive to strategic partners (APIs, dashboards, audit trails).

### 11.2 Strategic Partner Ecosystem (Five Partner Types)

Cuboid will engage five categories of strategic partners. Each has a different role, incentive, and integration model.

#### 11.2.1 Partner Type 1: Licensed BDCs (Core Partners)

**Role:** Compliance anchor, liquidity providers, distribution endpoints.

**Why they partner:** Access to broker-driven volume, inter-BDC trading, compliance automation.

**Integration model:** BDC Management Module (Section 12\) – monthly subscription plus transaction fees.

**Incentives:**

- Lower transaction fees for high-volume BDCs  
- Free compliance automation for first 3 months  
- Priority placement in broker inventory feed

**Outreach strategy:** Direct sales to BDC associations (ABCON), referrals from brokers, targeted outreach to high-volume BDCs in Lagos and Kano.

#### 11.2.2 Partner Type 2: Brokers (Volume Drivers – Informal)

**Role:** Volume drivers, customer relationships, last-mile distribution.

**Why they partner (even informally):** Productivity tools (chat-to-trade, quotes, customer management), access to BDC inventory, light escrow.

**Integration model:** Broker mode (free, with transaction fees). No formal partnership agreement required – brokers sign up individually.

**Incentives:**

- Lower transaction fees for high volume  
- Referral fees for bringing BDCs to platform  
- "Trusted broker" badge after 500 successful trades

**Outreach strategy:** WhatsApp groups, bank worker networks, word-of-mouth, referral bonuses.

#### 11.2.3 Partner Type 3: Commercial Banks (Settlement & Compliance)

**Role:** Settlement infrastructure, BDC account verification, potential FX source.

**Why they partner:** Reduce BDC compliance monitoring burden, gain visibility into BDC activity, earn settlement fees.

**Integration model:** API-based settlement confirmation, read-only access to BDC compliance data (with BDC permission).

**Incentives:**

- Settlement fee share  
- Reduced manual monitoring of BDC accounts  
- Preferential relationship with compliant BDCs

**Outreach strategy:** Approach bank treasury departments and compliance units. Pitch: "We give you visibility and reduce your liability. You give us settlement rails."

#### 11.2.4 Partner Type 4: Fintechs & PSPs (API Customers)

**Role:** Distribute FX to their customers via Cuboid's BDC network.

**Why they partner:** Access to compliant BDC network without building their own.

**Integration model:** API access (Phase 3\) – fintech integrates Cuboid's FX rates and execution into their app.

**Incentives:**

- Revenue share on FX transactions  
- White-label options for large partners

**Outreach strategy:** Target fintechs that already serve SMEs or have international payment needs (e.g., Paystack, Flutterwave, Moniepoint).

#### 11.2.5 Partner Type 5: Regulators (CBN, NFIU) – Compliance Allies

**Role:** Provide regulatory legitimacy, sandbox access, potential formal recognition.

**Why they partner:** Gain visibility into previously invisible FX flows, reduce supervision cost, access audit trails.

**Integration model:** Regulator dashboard (read-only, aggregated by default, drill-down available upon request).

**Incentives:**

- Free dashboard access  
- Data on broker-driven volume (previously invisible)  
- Pathway to formalize informal brokers

**Outreach strategy:** Proactive engagement. Approach CBN and NFIU with a "we want to help" message, not a "please approve us" request. Offer sandbox participation.

### 11.3 Compliance Module: Features for Regulator Readiness

The Compliance Module is the set of features that makes Cuboid acceptable to regulators. It is built incrementally but designed from Day 1\.

#### 11.3.1 Feature: Audit Trail (MVP)

**Description:** Every action on the platform is logged immutably: signups, logins, trade requests, quotes, customer additions, settlement confirmations.

**Data captured per event:**

| Field | Example |
| :---- | :---- |
| Timestamp | 2025-01-15 10:32:45 UTC |
| User ID | broker\_789abc |
| User role | broker (Rung 2\) |
| Action type | trade\_request |
| Action details | {"amount":5000, "currency":"USD", "purpose":"school\_fees"} |
| IP address (hashed) | a1b2c3d4e5f6... |
| Session ID | sess\_123xyz |

**Regulator value:** Any disputed transaction or suspicious activity can be reconstructed. Auditor can request data and receive complete logs.

#### 11.3.2 Feature: Licensed Counterparty Requirement (MVP)

**Description:** The platform does not allow broker-to-broker anonymous trading. Any trade execution (not just request) must involve at least one licensed BDC.

**Enforcement:**

- System checks BDC verification status before allowing trade finalization  
- Brokers cannot mark a trade as complete without selecting a licensed BDC counterparty  
- Attempts to bypass are logged and flagged

**Regulator value:** Prevents Cuboid from becoming a platform for unlicensed FX dealing. Every completed trade has a regulated entity on one side.

#### 11.3.3 Feature: Transaction Limits by Verification Tier (MVP)

**Description:** Users at different compliance ladder rungs have different transaction limits.

| Rung | Max Trade Request (USD) | Max Trade Execution (USD) | Daily Volume Limit |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| 1 (Anonymous) | None (view only) | None | N/A |
| 2 (Registered) | $1,000 | $0 (cannot execute) | N/A |
| 3 (Verified ID) | $10,000 | $5,000 (via BDC partner) | $20,000 |
| 4 (BDC-partnered) | $50,000 | $50,000 | $200,000 |
| 5 (Licensed BDC) | Unlimited | Unlimited | CBN guidelines |

**Regulator value:** Prevents large-scale unlicensed activity. Encourages users to climb the compliance ladder.

#### 11.3.4 Feature: Compliance Nudge Engine (MVP)

**Description:** Automated messages encouraging users to formalize as they reach volume thresholds.

**Nudge triggers:**

| Trigger | Nudge |
| :---- | :---- |
| 10 trade requests | "You're using Cuboid actively. Partner with a BDC to increase your limits." |
| $50k total volume | "You've moved over $50k. Formalize your status to reduce risk." |
| 30 days active | "30 days on Cuboid\! Here's how to partner with a BDC." |
| 5 failed trades (settlement) | "Settlement failures are risky. Light escrow available with ID verification." |

**Regulator value:** Demonstrates proactive effort to convert informal users to formal channels.

#### 11.3.5 Feature: Manual Compliance Export (MVP – Phase 1\)

**Description:** BDCs can export transaction data in CBN/NFIU-compliant format for manual filing.

**Export formats:**

- CSV matching CBN daily return template  
- Excel with pre-filled tabs for weekly positions  
- JSON for technical users

**Regulator value:** Immediate compliance improvement over manual Excel entry. Automated filing (Phase 2\) is the next step.

#### 11.3.6 Feature: Automated Compliance Filing (Phase 2\)

**Description:** One-click (or API-push) submission of compliance reports to CBN and NFIU.

| Report | Auto-populated from | Submission method |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Daily returns | Trades logged that day | Email to CBN (initially), API (future) |
| Weekly positions | Inventory snapshot | Email to CBN |
| CTRs (Currency Transaction Reports) | Trades \> $1,000 | goAML format, email or API |
| STRs (Suspicious Transaction Reports) | Flagged by system \+ BDC review | goAML format |

**Regulator value:** BDCs using Cuboid will have near-perfect compliance. Regulators receive clean, timely, accurate data.

#### 11.3.7 Feature: Internal Regulator Dashboard (Phase 2 – Shared in Phase 3\)

**Description:** Web-based dashboard showing aggregated platform activity, available to CBN/NFIU upon agreement.

**Dashboard views:**

| View | Data | Anonymization |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Summary | Total volume, active BDCs, active brokers, rate trends | Fully aggregated |
| Geographic | Volume by city, state | Aggregated |
| BDC compliance | % filing on time, average filing delay | Aggregated (no BDC names) |
| Suspicious activity | Number of flagged transactions, types | Aggregated |
| Drill-down (by request) | Individual BDC or broker data | Requires formal request |

**Regulator value:** Real-time visibility into previously invisible FX flows. Enables data-driven policy.

### 11.4 Partner Incentive Structures

#### 11.4.1 BDC Incentives

| Volume Tier (Monthly) | Transaction Fee | Subscription Discount | Other Benefits |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| \< $100k | 0.3% | None | Standard support |
| $100k – $500k | 0.25% | 10% off subscription | Priority support |
| $500k – $1M | 0.2% | 25% off subscription | Featured in broker feed |
| \> $1M | 0.15% | 50% off subscription | Dedicated account manager |

#### 11.4.2 Broker Incentives (Informal)

| Volume Tier (Monthly) | Transaction Fee | Referral Bonus (per BDC) | Badge |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| \< $50k | 0.3% | 5% of BDC sub for 6 months | None |
| $50k – $200k | 0.25% | 10% of BDC sub for 12 months | "Trusted Broker" |
| \> $200k | 0.2% | 15% of BDC sub for 12 months | "Premium Broker" |

**Referral bonus example:** Broker refers a BDC that pays $50/month for BDC Management Module. Broker earns $5–$7.50 per month for 6–12 months. Passive income incentive.

#### 11.4.3 Bank Incentives

| Bank Contribution | Cuboid Offer |
| :---- | :---- |
| Provide settlement accounts for Cuboid escrow | Revenue share on transaction fees |
| Offer preferential rates to Cuboid BDCs | Brand placement on BDC dashboard |
| Integrate settlement confirmation API | Reduced BDC compliance monitoring burden |
| Become FX source for Cuboid BDCs | Access to BDC network for retail distribution |

#### 11.4.4 Fintech Incentives

| Fintech Volume (Monthly) | API Fee | Transaction Fee |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| \< $100k | $500/month | 0.3% |
| $100k – $1M | $1,000/month | 0.25% |
| \> $1M | $2,000/month | 0.2% |

### 11.5 Regulator Engagement Roadmap

Cubido will not wait for regulators to come to Cuboid. Cuboid will approach regulators proactively.

| Phase | Timing | Action | Expected Outcome |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Phase 1: Information** | Month 2 | Share concept note with CBN Fintech Desk. Describe broker-aware strategy, compliance ladder, licensed counterparty requirement. | No objection to pilot. |
| **Phase 2: Sandbox application** | Month 4 | Apply for CBN Regulatory Sandbox (if available). Emphasize visibility into informal flows. | Sandbox acceptance or no-objection letter. |
| **Phase 3: Dashboard demo** | Month 6 | Demo internal regulator dashboard to CBN/NFIU. Show aggregated data from pilot. | Interest in formal dashboard access. |
| **Phase 4: Formal partnership** | Month 12 | Sign MOU with CBN/NFIU for data sharing. Offer free dashboard access. | Regulatory recognition as compliance utility. |
| **Phase 5: API integration** | Month 18 | Integrate with NFIU goAML for automated filing. | Full regulatory integration. |

**Key message to regulators (repeated):**

"We see the same problem you see: 80% of retail FX volume is invisible. We have built a platform that makes that invisibility visible, without destroying the trust and speed that customers value. Work with us."

### 11.6 Compliance Risk Mitigation Matrix

| Risk | Mitigation | Owner |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Regulator views Cuboid as facilitating unlicensed trading | Licensed counterparty requirement; terms of service; proactive engagement | Legal \+ Compliance Lead |
| Banks refuse to settle broker-BDC trades | Partner with banks early; demonstrate compliance controls | Partnerships Lead |
| BDCs refuse to work with brokers (seen as competitors) | Show BDCs volume opportunity; broker demand feed; revenue share | Product \+ Sales |
| Brokers use platform for money laundering | Transaction limits; suspicious activity flagging; audit trails | Compliance Lead |
| Data privacy concerns (broker customer lists) | Customer data owned by broker; Cuboid does not sell or share without permission | Legal \+ Product |

### 11.7 Go-to-Market Phases with Compliance Milestones

| Phase | Timing | GTM Activity | Compliance Milestone |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Phase 0: Stealth** | Months 0–3 | Recruit 20–30 brokers (bank worker networks). No public launch. | Audit trail active; terms of service in place. |
| **Phase 1: Pilot** | Months 3–6 | Onboard 5–10 BDCs. Enable broker-BDC trades. Limited to Lagos. | Licensed counterparty rule enforced; manual compliance export available. |
| **Phase 2: Soft Launch** | Months 6–9 | Expand to 50 brokers, 25 BDCs. Add Kano, Abuja. | Compliance ladder active (Rungs 1-4); nudge engine live. |
| **Phase 3: Regulator Engagement** | Months 9–12 | Demo dashboard to CBN/NFIU. Apply for sandbox or no-objection letter. | Internal regulator dashboard built; data sharing agreement offered. |
| **Phase 4: Scale** | Months 12–18 | Expand to 500 brokers, 100 BDCs. Add API for fintechs. | Automated compliance filing (Phase 2); regulator dashboard shared. |

### 11.8 Success Metrics for GTM & Compliance Module

| Metric | Target (Month 12\) | Target (Month 18\) |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Active brokers on platform | 500 | 2,000 |
| Active BDCs on platform | 50 | 200 |
| Monthly transaction volume | $5M – $10M | $20M – $50M |
| Brokers who have climbed to Rung 3+ (verified) | 20% | 40% |
| Brokers who have climbed to Rung 4+ (BDC-partnered) | 5% | 15% |
| BDCs using automated compliance (Phase 2\) | N/A (Phase 2 starts Month 12\) | 50% of active BDCs |
| Regulator sandbox/no-objection letter status | Applied or accepted | Obtained |
| Monthly recurring revenue (subscriptions \+ fees) | $5,000 – $15,000 | $20,000 – $50,000 |

---

## SECTION 12: BDC MANAGEMENT MODULE – SELLABLE TO PARTNERS

### 12.1 Overview: The Product That BDCs Pay For

The BDC Management Module is the primary **sellable product** for licensed BDCs. While brokers drive volume, BDCs pay monthly subscriptions. This module is the revenue anchor for Cuboid's business model.

**Positioning:** "Digitize your BDC operations for less than the cost of one compliance fine."

**Price:** $20–$100 per month depending on volume and features. This is deliberately affordable – lower than any comparable software, and far lower than the cost of a compliance officer or fines.

### 12.2 Core Features (All Included in Base Subscription)

#### 12.2.1 Feature: Real-Time Inventory Dashboard

**Description:** A single view of all currency holdings across all branches.

**What BDC sees:**

- USD balance (total and by branch)  
- NGN balance  
- Other currencies (GBP, EUR) if applicable  
- Recent inflows/outflows  
- Idle inventory alert (USD held \>3 days without sale)

**Value to BDC:** No more Excel spreadsheets or end-of-day manual counts. Know position instantly.

#### 12.2.2 Feature: Customer Management & KYC Storage

**Description:** Digital storage of customer information and transaction history.

**What BDC sees:**

- Customer name, contact, ID type/number  
- Transaction history (dates, amounts, rates, purposes)  
- KYC documents (photo of ID, customer photo)  
- Notes (e.g., "prefers large denominations")

**Value to BDC:** Audit-ready KYC. Faster service for repeat customers. No lost paperwork.

#### 12.2.3 Feature: Digital Receipt Generation

**Description:** Generate CBN-compliant receipts instantly with QR code.

**What BDC sees:**

- Input amount and customer details  
- System generates printable/sharable receipt  
- QR code links to transaction record in Cuboid (for auditor)

**Value to BDC:** Compliant receipts in seconds. No handwritten receipts. Auditor can verify instantly.

#### 12.2.4 Feature: Inter-BDC Trading

**Description:** See excess/deficit inventory from other BDCs on platform and execute peer trades.

**What BDC sees:**

- "Excess inventory" feed (BDCs selling USD)  
- "Demand" feed (BDCs buying USD)  
- Accept offers or post own offers  
- Settlement tracking

**Value to BDC:** Balance inventory without phone calls. Reduce idle USD. Never turn away a customer due to shortage.

#### 12.2.5 Feature: Broker Demand Feed

**Description:** See trade requests from brokers in your area (postcode or city).

**What BDC sees:**

- "Broker in Ikeja needs $5k USD for school fees"  
- Distance from BDC shop  
- Broker reputation score (based on past trades)

**Value to BDC:** New revenue channel. Access to broker-driven volume without manual outreach.

#### 12.2.6 Feature: Transaction History & Audit Trail

**Description:** Complete log of every transaction, searchable and exportable.

**What BDC sees:**

- All trades (customer, broker, inter-BDC)  
- Settlement status (pending, completed, failed)  
- Export to Excel/CSV for internal reporting

**Value to BDC:** No more shoebox of receipts. Regulator requests? Export and send in minutes.

### 12.3 Add-On Features (Additional Fee)

#### 12.3.1 Add-On: Compliance Automation (Phase 2\)

**Price:** $10–$30 per month

**Features:**

- Auto-generated CBN daily returns  
- Auto-generated weekly positions  
- One-click filing (or API push)  
- STR/CTR assistance (flagging \+ template)

**Value to BDC:** Save 10–20 hours per week. Avoid fines for late/incorrect filing. Compliance officer not required.

#### 12.3.2 Add-On: Multi-Branch Support

**Price:** $20 per additional branch per month (first branch included)

**Features:**

- Separate inventory per branch  
- Branch-level reporting  
- Transfers between branches tracked  
- Consolidated HQ dashboard

**Value to BDC:** Medium/large BDCs with multiple locations can manage centrally.

#### 12.3.3 Add-On: API Access (for BDCs with fintech partners)

**Price:** $50–$200 per month

**Features:**

- API for BDC to integrate with their own systems  
- Webhooks for trade notifications  
- Custom reporting endpoints

**Value to BDC:** BDCs that serve fintech partners can automate integration.

### 12.4 Pricing Tiers

| Tier | Monthly Price | Features | Target BDC |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Lite** | $20 | Inventory, customer mgmt (100 customers), digital receipts, basic reports | Small BDC (\<$500k monthly volume) |
| **Pro** | $50 | Lite \+ inter-BDC trading, broker demand feed, 500 customers, transaction export | Medium BDC ($500k–$2M monthly volume) |
| **Enterprise** | $100 | Pro \+ multi-branch (3 branches included), compliance automation, priority support | Large BDC (\>$2M monthly volume) |

**Volume discounts:**

- 10% off for annual prepayment  
- Additional 10% off for BDCs with \>$1M monthly volume on platform

### 12.5 Value Proposition to BDCs (ROI Calculation)

**Cost of BDC Management Module (Pro tier):** $50/month \= $600/year

**Value delivered:**

| Benefit | Estimated Annual Value | Calculation |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Reduced compliance labor | $2,400 – $12,000 | Saves 5–20 hours/week at $10/hour |
| Avoided compliance fines | $1,000 – $5,000 | Typical fines for late/incorrect filing |
| Inter-BDC trading savings | $2,000 – $10,000 | Reduces idle inventory; better rates |
| Broker channel revenue | $5,000 – $50,000 | New volume from brokers on platform |
| Operational efficiency | $1,000 – $5,000 | Less manual work, fewer errors |
| **Total estimated value** | **$11,400 – $82,000** |  |

**ROI:** For $600/year, BDC gains at least $11,000 in value. **18x ROI** at conservative estimate.

### 12.6 BDC Onboarding Process

| Step | Action | Owner | Timeline |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| 1 | BDC expresses interest (website, referral, broker) | Sales | Day 0 |
| 2 | Demo (15-min screen share or recorded video) | Sales | Day 1 |
| 3 | KYB verification (upload license, CAC, director IDs) | Compliance | Day 1-2 |
| 4 | Subscription payment (card or bank transfer) | BDC | Day 2 |
| 5 | Account setup (branches, users, permissions) | Support | Day 2-3 |
| 6 | Training (recorded videos \+ optional call) | Support | Day 3 |
| 7 | Go-live (first trade or inventory entry) | BDC | Day 3-5 |

**Target:** From expression of interest to first trade within 5 days.

### 12.7 BDC Retention Strategy

| Retention Lever | Description | Target Impact |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Volume-based discounts | Lower transaction fees as volume grows | Increase switching cost |
| Compliance value | BDC becomes dependent on automated filing | High stickiness |
| Network effects | Inter-BDC trading only valuable if other BDCs are on platform | Self-reinforcing |
| Broker demand | Brokers only send requests to BDCs on platform | Demand-side stickiness |
| Annual prepay discount | 10% off for annual commitment | Lock-in |
| Feature release cadence | New features monthly; BDCs stay for updates | Engagement |

### 12.8 BDC Segmentation for Sales

| Segment | Count (Est.) | Target Adoption (Year 1\) | Sales Approach |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Large BDCs (\>$2M monthly volume) | 200–300 | 10% (20–30) | Direct sales, enterprise pricing, dedicated support |
| Medium BDCs ($500k–$2M) | 500–800 | 10% (50–80) | Direct sales \+ webinar demos |
| Small BDCs (\<$500k) | 3,000–4,000 | 2% (60–80) | Self-serve, referral from brokers |
| **Total** | **4,000–5,000** | **130–190** |  |

### 12.9 Competitive Positioning Against Alternatives

| Alternative | Cost | Features | Why Cuboid Wins |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Excel/paper | Free (but labor-intensive) | None | Automation, compliance, network effects |
| Custom software (e.g., Finacle) | $5,000+ upfront \+ monthly | Inventory, receipts | Cuboid is 1/10th the cost; includes network |
| Bank-provided portals | Free (but bank-specific) | Limited (reporting only) | Cuboid is BDC-owned, not bank-dependent |
| Manual (nothing) | Free | None | Cuboid saves time and reduces fines |

### 12.10 BDC Management Module Roadmap

| Feature | MVP (Month 3\) | Phase 2 (Month 6-9) | Phase 3 (Month 12-18) |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Inventory dashboard | Yes (basic) | Yes (branch-level) | Yes (predictive) |
| Customer management | Yes (100 customers) | Yes (500 customers) | Yes (unlimited \+ analytics) |
| Digital receipts | Yes (basic) | Yes (QR code) | Yes (API for printing) |
| Inter-BDC trading | Yes (manual matching) | Yes (auto-matching) | Yes (price discovery) |
| Broker demand feed | Yes (view only) | Yes (accept/decline) | Yes (automated response) |
| Compliance automation | Manual export | One-click filing | API to CBN/NFIU |
| Multi-branch | No | Yes (add-on) | Yes (included in Enterprise) |
| API access | No | No | Yes (add-on) |

### 12.11 Sales and Marketing for BDC Module

**Channels:**

| Channel | Description | Expected Conversion |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Broker referrals | Brokers earn commission for referring BDCs | High (trust-based) |
| Direct outreach | Call/visit BDCs in Lagos, Kano, Abuja | Medium |
| BDC associations (ABCON) | Partner for member outreach | Medium-High |
| Digital marketing | Google/Facebook ads targeting "BDC software" | Low (but scalable) |
| Regulator recommendation | If CBN endorses Cuboid for compliance | Very High |

**Sales collateral needed:**

- One-page ROI flyer ("Save $10,000/year for $50/month")  
- 5-minute demo video  
- Comparison sheet vs Excel/manual  
- Testimonial from pilot BDC (once available)

### 12.12 BDC Management Module Financial Projections

| Metric | Year 1 | Year 2 | Year 3 |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| BDCs on platform (cumulative) | 50 | 250 | 600 |
| Average subscription ($/month) | $40 | $45 | $50 |
| Monthly subscription revenue | $2,000 | $11,250 | $30,000 |
| Annual subscription revenue | $24,000 | $135,000 | $360,000 |
| Add-on revenue (compliance, multi-branch) | $2,000 | $20,000 | $60,000 |
| **Total BDC module revenue** | **$26,000** | **$155,000** | **$420,000** |

**Note:** These projections assume no significant seed round before Year 2\. With a $50k–$100k seed round at Month 12, growth would accelerate.

### 12.13 BDC Module as a Standalone Product (Optional)

While Cuboid is designed as an integrated platform (brokers \+ BDCs together), the BDC Management Module **could** be sold as a standalone product to BDCs who do not want broker integration.

**Standalone version features:**

- Inventory management  
- Customer management \+ KYC  
- Digital receipts  
- Compliance reporting (manual export)  
- No inter-BDC trading (requires network)  
- No broker demand feed

**Price:** $30–$50/month (slightly lower than full version)

**Pros of standalone:** Can sell to BDCs who are not ready for broker integration. Lower barrier to entry.

**Cons of standalone:** Loses network effects. BDCs get less value. Less differentiation from competitors.

**Recommendation:** Offer standalone as an entry tier, but aggressively upsell to full platform (which includes inter-BDC trading and broker feed). The network is the moat.

**End of Section 11 and Section 12**

I have now completed **Section 11 (GTM & Compliance Module – Strategic Partners \+ BDCs)** and **Section 12 (BDC Management Module – Sellable to Partners)**.

Shall I proceed with **Section 13 (The Broker Bridge – Features That Attract Informal Operators Without Legitimizing Illegality)** and **Section 14 (Phased GTM Plan – Broker-First, BDC-Second)** next?

Here is **Section 13** and **Section 14** of the Cuboid Business Concept Note, continuing from where we left off. Formatted for Google Docs copy-paste.
