## SECTION 26: APPENDIX F – INSANE TECHNOLOGIES – STRATEGIC ROLE & EQUITY JUSTIFICATION

### F.1 Overview: The Strategic Partner

Insane Technologies is not a passive investor. It is a **strategic partner** that holds a minimum of 25% equity in Cuboid in exchange for significant technical infrastructure, strategic guidance, and network access. This appendix details the rationale, valuation, and terms of this partnership.

**The core proposition:** Cuboid is built *on* Insane Technologies' existing infrastructure, not from scratch. This reduces development time from 12+ months to 3 months and cash requirements from $50,000+ to $5,500.

### F.2 Insane Technologies – Company Background

| Aspect | Detail |
| :---- | :---- |
| Name | Insane Technologies |
| Primary business | Fintech infrastructure, developer tools, API services |
| Key products | Authentication service, chat engine, ledger system, API gateway |
| Track record | \[Insert relevant track record – e.g., number of clients, years in operation, notable deployments\] |
| Geographic focus | Nigeria / West Africa |
| Strategic assets | Pre-built modules, developer team, banking relationships |

### F.3 Contribution to Cuboid (Detailed Valuation)

#### F.3.1 Technical Infrastructure Provided

| Component | Description | Replacement Cost (USD) | Cuboid Savings |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| **Authentication service** | Phone/OTP, JWT, session management, role-based access control | $5,000 – $8,000 | 100% |
| **Real-time chat engine** | WebSocket-based messaging for chat-to-trade feature | $8,000 – $12,000 | 100% |
| **Basic ledger system** | Double-entry transaction logging, balance tracking | $3,000 – $5,000 | 100% |
| **API gateway / scaffolding** | Routes, middleware, error handling, logging, rate limiting | $3,000 – $6,000 | 100% |
| **Notification service** | SMS, email, in-app notifications (Twilio integration) | $2,000 – $4,000 | 100% |
| **Infrastructure as code** | Terraform/CloudFormation templates for deployment | $2,000 – $6,000 | 100% |
| **Developer hours saved** | Estimated 500-800 hours of development time | $10,000 – $20,000 | 100% |
| **Total contributed value** |  | **$33,000 – $61,000** |  |

**Midpoint valuation:** \~$47,000

#### F.3.2 Strategic Guidance & Advisory

| Contribution | Description | Estimated Value |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Technical architecture review | Monthly advisory on scalability, security, best practices | $10,000 – $20,000 (annualized) |
| Product roadmap input | Strategic direction, feature prioritization | $5,000 – $10,000 (annualized) |
| Regulatory navigation | Guidance on CBN/NFIU engagement, compliance approach | $5,000 – $10,000 |
| Network access | Introductions to BDC associations, bank contacts, potential investors | $10,000 – $25,000 |
| **Total strategic value (Year 1\)** |  | **$30,000 – $65,000** |

#### F.3.3 Total Contribution (Year 1\)

| Category | Low Estimate | High Estimate |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Technical infrastructure | $33,000 | $61,000 |
| Strategic guidance | $30,000 | $65,000 |
| **Total Year 1 contribution** | **$63,000** | **$126,000** |

**Midpoint:** \~$94,500

### F.4 Equity Justification

| Metric | Value |
| :---- | :---- |
| Insane Technologies equity | **Minimum 25%** |
| Valuation of contribution (Year 1\) | $63,000 – $126,000 |
| Implied valuation of Cuboid (based on contribution) | $252,000 – $504,000 |
| Cash funding from strategic round | $5,500 |
| Total Cuboid value (cash \+ contribution) | $257,500 – $509,500 |

**Conclusion:** 25% equity for a \~$95,000 contribution implies a Cuboid valuation of \~$380,000 – which is reasonable for a pre-revenue fintech platform with significant infrastructure already in place.

### F.5 Equity Terms Summary

| Term | Detail |
| :---- | :---- |
| Equity stake | Minimum 25% of fully diluted shares |
| Form of contribution | Technology (pre-built modules), strategic guidance, network access. No cash required. |
| Valuation of contribution | $63,000 – $126,000 (Year 1\) |
| Vesting schedule | 4-year vesting, 1-year cliff. 25% vests after 1 year; remaining monthly thereafter. |
| Board representation | Right to appoint one director to Cuboid board |
| Anti-dilution | Participation rights in future equity rounds to maintain minimum 25% (pro-rata) |
| Transfer restrictions | Cannot transfer equity without founder consent for first 2 years |
| ROFR (Right of First Refusal) | Cuboid has ROFR on any proposed transfer |
| Drag-along rights | Insane Technologies agrees to drag-along in acquisition (standard) |
| Tag-along rights | Insane Technologies has tag-along rights in acquisition |
| IP license | Perpetual, royalty-free license to contributed modules for Cuboid |
| Termination condition | License terminates if Insane Technologies' equity falls below 15% without consent |

### F.6 Comparison to Typical Investor Contributions

| Investor Type | Cash Contribution | Non-Cash Contribution | Equity Typical | Cuboid Case |
| :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Angel investor | $25k – $100k | Minimal | 5% – 15% | N/A |
| VC (Seed) | $500k – $2M | Strategic guidance | 20% – 30% | N/A |
| Strategic partner | $0 – $50k | Technology, network, expertise | 10% – 30% | ✓ |
| Insane Technologies | $0 cash | $63k – $126k (tech \+ strategy) | 25% | ✓ |

**Conclusion:** Insane Technologies' 25% equity is consistent with strategic partner benchmarks, especially given the significant technology contribution.

### F.7 Alignment of Incentives

| Party | Incentive | How Equity Aligns |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Insane Technologies | Cuboid succeeds → contributed modules gain adoption → Insane Technologies benefits | 25% equity ensures Insane Technologies is motivated to support Cuboid long-term |
| Cuboid | Access to infrastructure without cash outlay → faster launch, lower risk | Insane Technologies' equity is tied to Cuboid's success |
| Founders | Build valuable company | Majority equity (50-65%) |
| Strategic investors | High ROI on small investment | 5-15% equity at over-discounted valuation |

**No misalignment:** All parties benefit when Cuboid grows.

### F.8 Risk Mitigation (Insane Technologies Relationship)

| Risk | Mitigation |
| :---- | :---- |
| Insane Technologies fails to deliver promised modules | Written agreement with deliverables; intellectual property assignment |
| Insane Technologies becomes unresponsive | Clear communication expectations (monthly calls); backup open-source solutions available |
| Equity dispute | Shareholders' agreement with clear valuation, vesting, and dispute resolution |
| Insane Technologies sells equity to competitor | ROFR; transfer restrictions for first 2 years |
| Insane Technologies' reputation damages Cuboid | Due diligence on Insane Technologies before agreement; right to terminate for reputational harm |

### F.9 Intellectual Property Ownership

| IP Asset | Owner | Terms |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Pre-existing Insane Technologies modules (auth, chat, ledger, API scaffolding) | Insane Technologies | Perpetual, royalty-free license to Cuboid |
| Cuboid-specific code (trade engine, inventory mgmt, compliance features) | Cuboid Technologies Ltd. | Full ownership |
| Modifications to Insane Technologies modules made for Cuboid | Cuboid Technologies Ltd. | Cuboid owns modifications; licenses back to Insane Technologies non-exclusively |
| Cuboid brand, logo, name | Cuboid Technologies Ltd. | Full ownership |
| Compliance ladder methodology | Cuboid Technologies Ltd. | Trade secret (not shared) |

### F.10 Governance and Decision-Making

| Decision Type | Approval Required | Insane Technologies Role |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Day-to-day operations | CEO | No approval needed |
| Annual budget | Board majority | One board vote |
| New equity issuance (dilution) | Board majority \+ Insane Technologies consent if dilution below 20% | Veto right |
| Acquisition of Cuboid | Board majority \+ shareholder vote | One board vote; tag-along rights |
| Debt \>$50,000 | Board majority | One board vote |
| Change to Insane Technologies equity terms | Unanimous consent (including Insane Technologies) | Veto right |

### F.11 Exit Scenarios

| Scenario | Insane Technologies Outcome | Cuboid Outcome |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Acquisition ($10M) | 25% \= $2.5M | Positive return for all shareholders |
| Acquisition ($50M) | 25% \= $12.5M | Strong return |
| Acquisition ($200M – e.g., Paystack-style) | 25% \= $50M | Exceptional return |
| IPO | 25% of public shares | Liquidity event |
| Cuboid winds down | Loss of contributed technology (already amortized) | Minimal cash loss ($5,500) |

### F.12 Relationship Governance

| Aspect | Frequency | Method |
| :---- | :---- | :---- |
| Board meetings | Quarterly (formal) | Video conference \+ written minutes |
| Operational updates | Weekly | Email or chat |
| Technical sync (dev team) | Bi-weekly | Video call |
| Annual strategic review | Yearly | In-person (if feasible) |
| Conflict resolution | As needed | Escalate to board; arbitration if unresolved |

### F.13 Why 25% Is Fair (Summary)

| Reason | Explanation |
| :---- | :---- |
| **Significant technology contribution** | $63k – $126k in Year 1 value (auth, chat, ledger, API, dev hours saved) |
| **Speed to market** | Without Insane Technologies, Cuboid would need 12+ months and $50k+ to build from scratch |
| **Ongoing strategic value** | Monthly advisory, network access, regulatory guidance |
| **Risk sharing** | Insane Technologies takes equity risk (no cash return if Cuboid fails) |
| **Market precedent** | Strategic partners typically receive 10-30% for similar contributions |
| **Founder retention** | Insane Technologies' 25% leaves 50-65% for founders – founders remain majority |

### F.14 Key Agreement Clauses (Shareholders' Agreement)

**Clause 1: Vesting**

"Insane Technologies' 25% equity stake shall vest ratably over 48 months, with 25% vesting upon the first anniversary of this Agreement (the 'Cliff'), and the remaining 75% vesting in equal monthly installments over the subsequent 36 months. Upon a Change of Control, all unvested equity shall accelerate and fully vest."

**Clause 2: Anti-Dilution**

"In the event Cuboid issues additional equity securities, Insane Technologies shall have the right to participate in such issuance on a pro-rata basis to maintain its minimum 25% ownership. If Insane Technologies elects not to participate, its ownership shall be diluted, but no anti-dilution adjustment shall apply."

**Clause 3: Board Representation**

"Insane Technologies shall have the right to appoint one (1) director to the Board of Directors of Cuboid. Such director shall have the same voting rights as other directors."

**Clause 4: Transfer Restrictions**

"For a period of 24 months from the date of this Agreement, Insane Technologies shall not transfer any of its equity in Cuboid without the prior written consent of the Founders. Thereafter, transfers shall be subject to a Right of First Refusal in favor of Cuboid."

**Clause 5: IP License**

"Insane Technologies hereby grants to Cuboid a perpetual, irrevocable, royalty-free, worldwide, non-exclusive license to use, modify, and distribute the contributed modules (authentication, chat engine, ledger, API scaffolding) for the purpose of operating the Cuboid platform. This license shall survive termination of this Agreement."

### F.15 Summary: Insane Technologies Strategic Role

| Element | Summary |
| :---- | :---- |
| **Role** | Strategic partner, not passive investor |
| **Equity** | Minimum 25% (floor, not ceiling) |
| **Contribution (Year 1\)** | $63k – $126k (technology \+ strategy) |
| **Cash from Insane Technologies** | $0 |
| **Vesting** | 4-year, 1-year cliff |
| **Board seat** | Yes (one director) |
| **Anti-dilution** | Pro-rata participation right |
| **IP license** | Perpetual, royalty-free to Cuboid |
| **Rationale** | Enables Cuboid to launch with $5,500 cash instead of $50k+ |

**Final note:** This appendix is provided for full transparency to strategic investors and regulators. The relationship between Cuboid and Insane Technologies is foundational to the Cuboid business model. Questions about this relationship should be directed to the Cuboid founder or Insane Technologies representative.

---

**End of Section 26 (Appendix F)**
